msg:Among the many choices, I stayed at Shunde Longju Hotel and was deeply impressed by its facilities and services. First of all, the breakfast buffet in this hotel is so rich! We have everything from Chinese pasta and porridge to American bacon, British desserts, juices, coffee, etc. Moreover, every dish is made very delicately, fully reflecting Shunde's pursuit of catering.

In addition, Shunde Longju Hotel also has a sky bar located on the upper floor - Luna. The name comes from the Spanish word for "moon," giving it a romantic feel. Luna Bar has indoor and outdoor areas, with the outdoor area offering unparalleled river views at night. Also, the drinks they serve are excellent and definitely worth a try.

Here I would also like to recommend the special and exquisite morning tea at Shunde Longju Hotel. The tea house dim sum is unique, not only exquisite and rich, but also integrated with the innovative ideas of the chefs. The new Chinese-style teahouse has an elegant and comfortable environment. Enjoying tea and snacks here is undoubtedly a refreshing and enjoyable experience.

The last thing to mention is that Shunde Longju Hotel has a heated swimming pool and a 24-hour fitness area. Whether you are on vacation or on a business trip, you can stay in perfect shape and exercise at any time here.

In short, Shunde Longju Hotel has become an accommodation choice worth recommending to everyone with its high-quality facilities and services such as Chinese and Western buffet breakfast, romantic sky bar, specialty exquisite morning tea, and constant-temperature swimming pool and fitness area. If you are looking for an accommodation experience that combines comfort and convenience, be sure to consider Shunde Longju Hotel!

msg:Summarize:

The prices of Longju and Haijunda Hilton are in the same price range, but there is a big gap in transportation, facilities, services, and room configuration. It is recommended that travelers consider it.

advantage:
1. The design of the hotel‚Äôs public areas is stylish and exquisite. The lobby bar, bar and cafeteria set up on the top floor are equipped with floor-to-ceiling windows, making you feel comfortable;
2. All-day dining restaurant, bar, indoor swimming pool, gym, and sauna facilities are in place. It‚Äôs OK to stay in the hotel on rainy days.

shortcoming:
1. Service awareness and attitude: There are no clear signs and guidance at the lobby entrance, and online car-hailing requires passengers to walk out of the hotel on their own; there is no greeting at the lobby entrance, nor active help with luggage;
2. The hotel has inconvenient transportation and few supporting facilities: The hotel is located on the edge of the Daliang and Ronggui business districts. You have to take a taxi to experience delicious food, and the transportation is not convenient.
3. Noise problem: There are construction sites around the hotel, and trucks occasionally pass by in the morning.
3. Defects in the soft furnishings in the room: Ordinary rooms are not equipped with armchairs, and the sofa has a straight backrest, which is as comfortable as a hard seat; the smart home experience is not good, for example, in sleep mode, if one person wakes up at night, the room will light up, waking up his companions. Suggested adjus**ents
4. Defects in the hard decoration in the room: The bathroom is not equipped with an exhaust fan, or the exhaust fan is too ineffective, making it difficult to discharge moisture after showering. Coupled with rainy days, the room is very humid and the living experience is poor.
